\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
C A\+PI\+: Character conversion. 

\doxysubsubsection*{Character Conversion C A\+PI}

This A\+PI is used to convert codepage or character encoded data to and from U\+T\+F-\/16. You can open a converter with \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a04af8743cca855974b87fd55a7970d6c}{ucnv\+\_\+open()}}. With that converter, you can get its properties, set options, convert your data and close the converter.

Since many software programs recognize different converter names for different types of converters, there are other functions in this A\+PI to iterate over the converter aliases. The functions \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a5b954cb4102add0e0400a149b37b3a9f}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Available\+Name()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a97c95bfc3450d7b3fcf8e1681f7b172c}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Alias()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_ab713bdfeeea22684aa5bbbf2e00d23ef}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Standard\+Name()}} are some of the more frequently used alias functions to get this information.

When a converter encounters an illegal, irregular, invalid or unmappable character its default behavior is to use a substitution character to replace the bad byte sequence. This behavior can be changed by using \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a304bcaa1f4cbc789d10197d6f51c94f1}{ucnv\+\_\+set\+From\+U\+Call\+Back()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afce4464cdb5b488460bf21c116cb1cf2}{ucnv\+\_\+set\+To\+U\+Call\+Back()}} on the converter. The header \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h}{ucnv\+\_\+err.\+h}} defines many other callback actions that can be used instead of a character substitution.

More information about this A\+PI can be found in our \href{http://icu-project.org/userguide/conversion.html}{\texttt{ User\textquotesingle{}s Guide}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{U\_CNV\_SAFECLONE\_BUFFERSIZE}{U\_CNV\_SAFECLONE\_BUFFERSIZE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define U\+\_\+\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+S\+A\+F\+E\+C\+L\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ZE~1024}

Definition of a buffer size that is designed to be large enough for converters to be cloned with \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aebb51e41917fe9b0488cfdb5717ff826}{ucnv\+\_\+safe\+Clone()}}. \begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000038}{Deprecated}}]I\+CU 52. Do not rely on \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aebb51e41917fe9b0488cfdb5717ff826}{ucnv\+\_\+safe\+Clone()}} cloning into any provided buffer. \end{DoxyRefDesc}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_aa3d7e4ae84f8a95b9735ed3491cdb77e}\label{ucnv_8h_aa3d7e4ae84f8a95b9735ed3491cdb77e}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!UCNV\_GET\_MAX\_BYTES\_FOR\_STRING@{UCNV\_GET\_MAX\_BYTES\_FOR\_STRING}}
\index{UCNV\_GET\_MAX\_BYTES\_FOR\_STRING@{UCNV\_GET\_MAX\_BYTES\_FOR\_STRING}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UCNV\_GET\_MAX\_BYTES\_FOR\_STRING}{UCNV\_GET\_MAX\_BYTES\_FOR\_STRING}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+T\+E\+S\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+NG(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{length,  }\item[{}]{max\+Char\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})~(((int32\+\_\+t)(length)+10)$\ast$(int32\+\_\+t)(max\+Char\+Size))}

Calculates the size of a buffer for conversion from Unicode to a charset. The calculated size is guaranteed to be sufficient for this conversion.

It takes into account initial and final non-\/character bytes that are output by some converters. It does not take into account callbacks which output more than one charset character sequence per call, like escape callbacks. The default (substitution) callback only outputs one charset character sequence.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em length} & Number of U\+Chars to be converted. \\
\hline
{\em max\+Char\+Size} & Return value from \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_ab284cb660babcd328f4e03f6f0b0b802}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Max\+Char\+Size()}} for the converter that will be used. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Size of a buffer that will be large enough to hold the output bytes of converting length U\+Chars with the converter that returned the max\+Char\+Size.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+S\+W\+A\+P\+\_\+\+L\+F\+N\+L\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+NG~\char`\"{},swaplfnl\char`\"{}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef void(U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 $\ast$ U\+Converter\+From\+U\+Callback) (const void $\ast$context, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_converter_from_unicode_args}{U\+Converter\+From\+Unicode\+Args}} $\ast$args, const \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$code\+Units, int32\+\_\+t length, \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}} code\+Point, \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a19e1a4d55a7679634e84b241b00de01a}{U\+Converter\+Callback\+Reason}} reason, \mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$p\+Error\+Code)}

Function pointer for error callback in the unicode to codepage direction. Called when an error has occurred in conversion from unicode, or on open/close of the callback (see reason). 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em context} & Pointer to the callback\textquotesingle{}s private data \\
\hline
{\em args} & Information about the conversion in progress \\
\hline
{\em code\+Units} & Points to \textquotesingle{}length\textquotesingle{} U\+Chars of the concerned Unicode sequence \\
\hline
{\em length} & Size (in bytes) of the concerned codepage sequence \\
\hline
{\em code\+Point} & Single U\+Char32 (U\+T\+F-\/32) containing the concerend Unicode codepoint. \\
\hline
{\em reason} & Defines the reason the callback was invoked \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & I\+CU error code in/out parameter. For converter callback functions, set to a conversion error before the call, and the callback may reset it to U\+\_\+\+Z\+E\+R\+O\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsection{Function Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a499316e130bdd073c394c92f55c315d2}\label{ucnv_8h_a499316e130bdd073c394c92f55c315d2}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_close@{ucnv\_close}}
\index{ucnv\_close@{ucnv\_close}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_close()}{ucnv\_close()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+close (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{converter }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Deletes the unicode converter and releases resources associated with just this instance. Does not free up shared converter tables.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_ad3f473f991769a94f21e195473470157}{ucnv\+\_\+openU}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a3f54f96fcedd8d89f433c4bd9437864d}{ucnv\+\_\+open\+C\+C\+S\+ID}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+0 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a8d23f178a9474210cce08530fbfe6ab3}\label{ucnv_8h_a8d23f178a9474210cce08530fbfe6ab3}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_compareNames@{ucnv\_compareNames}}
\index{ucnv\_compareNames@{ucnv\_compareNames}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_compareNames()}{ucnv\_compareNames()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+compare\+Names (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{name1,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{name2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Do a fuzzy compare of two converter/alias names. The comparison is case-\/insensitive, ignores leading zeroes if they are not followed by further digits, and ignores all but letters and digits. Thus the strings \char`\"{}\+U\+T\+F-\/8\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}utf\+\_\+8\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}u$\ast$\+T@f08\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}\+Utf 8\char`\"{} are exactly equivalent. See section 1.\+4, Charset Alias Matching in Unicode Technical Standard \#22 at \href{http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr22/}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+unicode.\+org/reports/tr22/}}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em name1} & a converter name or alias, zero-\/terminated \\
\hline
{\em name2} & a converter name or alias, zero-\/terminated \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if the names match, or a negative value if the name1 lexically precedes name2, or a positive value if the name1 lexically follows name2. @stable I\+CU 2.\+0 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a942e532c2f02bcaea39741d4b99764b5}\label{ucnv_8h_a942e532c2f02bcaea39741d4b99764b5}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_convert@{ucnv\_convert}}
\index{ucnv\_convert@{ucnv\_convert}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_convert()}{ucnv\_convert()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+convert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{to\+Converter\+Name,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{from\+Converter\+Name,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{target,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{target\+Capacity,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{source,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{source\+Length,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Convert from one external charset to another. Internally, two converters are opened according to the name arguments, then the text is converted to and from the 16-\/bit Unicode \char`\"{}pivot\char`\"{} using \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a1ab80dfe1f774537db9d5497a2ba8be7}{ucnv\+\_\+convert\+Ex()}}, then the converters are closed again.

This is a convenience function, not an efficient way to convert a lot of text\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a942e532c2f02bcaea39741d4b99764b5}{ucnv\+\_\+convert()}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item takes charset names, not converter objects, so that
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item two converters are opened for each call
\item only single-\/string conversion is possible, not streaming operation
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item does not provide enough information to find out, in case of failure, whether the to\+Unicode or the from\+Unicode conversion failed
\item allows N\+U\+L-\/terminated input (only a single N\+UL byte, will not work for charsets with multi-\/byte N\+U\+Ls) (if source\+Length==-\/1, see parameters)
\item terminate with a N\+UL on output (only a single N\+UL byte, not useful for charsets with multi-\/byte N\+U\+Ls), or set U\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+R\+M\+I\+N\+A\+T\+E\+D\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG if the output exactly fills the target buffer
\item a pivot buffer is provided internally
\end{DoxyItemize}

The function returns when one of the following is true\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the entire source text has been converted successfully to the target buffer and either the target buffer is terminated with a single N\+UL byte or the error code is set to U\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+R\+M\+I\+N\+A\+T\+E\+D\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG
\item a target buffer overflow occurred (U\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR) and the full output string length is returned (\char`\"{}preflighting\char`\"{})
\item a conversion error occurred (other \mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a4d202200b6aa6f3c965ea370e0c8155f}{U\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+R\+E()}}, see description of p\+Error\+Code)
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em to\+Converter\+Name} & The name of the converter that is used to convert from the U\+T\+F-\/16 pivot buffer to the target. \\
\hline
{\em from\+Converter\+Name} & The name of the converter that is used to convert from the source to the U\+T\+F-\/16 pivot buffer. \\
\hline
{\em target} & Pointer to the output buffer. \\
\hline
{\em target\+Capacity} & Capacity of the target, in bytes. \\
\hline
{\em source} & Pointer to the input buffer. \\
\hline
{\em source\+Length} & Length of the input text, in bytes, or -\/1 for N\+U\+L-\/terminated input. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & I\+CU error code in/out parameter. Must fulfill U\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS before the function call. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Length of the complete output text in bytes, even if it exceeds the target\+Capacity and a U\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR is set.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a1ab80dfe1f774537db9d5497a2ba8be7}\label{ucnv_8h_a1ab80dfe1f774537db9d5497a2ba8be7}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_convertEx@{ucnv\_convertEx}}
\index{ucnv\_convertEx@{ucnv\_convertEx}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_convertEx()}{ucnv\_convertEx()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+convert\+Ex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{target\+Cnv,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{source\+Cnv,  }\item[{char $\ast$$\ast$}]{target,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{target\+Limit,  }\item[{const char $\ast$$\ast$}]{source,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{source\+Limit,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$}]{pivot\+Start,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$$\ast$}]{pivot\+Source,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$$\ast$}]{pivot\+Target,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$}]{pivot\+Limit,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}}}]{reset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}}}]{flush,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Convert from one external charset to another using two existing U\+Converters. Internally, two conversions -\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa63cf11835833041f2ce0ed3662edfcd}{ucnv\+\_\+from\+Unicode()}} -\/ are used, \char`\"{}pivoting\char`\"{} through 16-\/bit Unicode.

Important\+: For streaming conversion (multiple function calls for successive parts of a text stream), the caller must provide a pivot buffer explicitly, and must preserve the pivot buffer and associated pointers from one call to another. (The buffer may be moved if its contents and the relative pointer positions are preserved.)

There is a similar function, \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a942e532c2f02bcaea39741d4b99764b5}{ucnv\+\_\+convert()}}, which has the following limitations\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item it takes charset names, not converter objects, so that
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item two converters are opened for each call
\item only single-\/string conversion is possible, not streaming operation
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item it does not provide enough information to find out, in case of failure, whether the to\+Unicode or the from\+Unicode conversion failed
\end{DoxyItemize}

By contrast, \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a1ab80dfe1f774537db9d5497a2ba8be7}{ucnv\+\_\+convert\+Ex()}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item takes U\+Converter parameters instead of charset names
\item fully exposes the pivot buffer for streaming conversion and complete error handling
\end{DoxyItemize}

\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a1ab80dfe1f774537db9d5497a2ba8be7}{ucnv\+\_\+convert\+Ex()}} also provides further convenience\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item an option to reset the converters at the beginning (if reset==true, see parameters; also sets $\ast$pivot\+Target=$\ast$pivot\+Source=pivot\+Start)
\item allow N\+U\+L-\/terminated input (only a single N\+UL byte, will not work for charsets with multi-\/byte N\+U\+Ls) (if source\+Limit==N\+U\+LL, see parameters)
\item terminate with a N\+UL on output (only a single N\+UL byte, not useful for charsets with multi-\/byte N\+U\+Ls), or set U\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+R\+M\+I\+N\+A\+T\+E\+D\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG if the output exactly fills the target buffer
\item the pivot buffer can be provided internally; possible only for whole-\/string conversion, not streaming conversion; in this case, the caller will not be able to get details about where an error occurred (if pivot\+Start==N\+U\+LL, see below)
\end{DoxyItemize}

The function returns when one of the following is true\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the entire source text has been converted successfully to the target buffer
\item a target buffer overflow occurred (U\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR)
\item a conversion error occurred (other \mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a4d202200b6aa6f3c965ea370e0c8155f}{U\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+R\+E()}}, see description of p\+Error\+Code)
\end{DoxyItemize}

Limitation compared to the direct use of \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa63cf11835833041f2ce0ed3662edfcd}{ucnv\+\_\+from\+Unicode()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode()}}\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a1ab80dfe1f774537db9d5497a2ba8be7}{ucnv\+\_\+convert\+Ex()}} does not provide offset information.

Limitation compared to \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a2cc3d9d8fbab664493a9aa189d120571}{ucnv\+\_\+from\+U\+Chars()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afd107e398535c523d900f030df8326df}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+U\+Chars()}}\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a1ab80dfe1f774537db9d5497a2ba8be7}{ucnv\+\_\+convert\+Ex()}} does not support preflighting directly.

Sample code for converting a single string from one external charset to U\+T\+F-\/8, ignoring the location of errors\+:

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em target\+Cnv} & Output converter, used to convert from the U\+T\+F-\/16 pivot to the target using \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa63cf11835833041f2ce0ed3662edfcd}{ucnv\+\_\+from\+Unicode()}}. \\
\hline
{\em source\+Cnv} & Input converter, used to convert from the source to the U\+T\+F-\/16 pivot using \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode()}}. \\
\hline
{\em target} & I/O parameter, same as for \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a2cc3d9d8fbab664493a9aa189d120571}{ucnv\+\_\+from\+U\+Chars()}}. Input\+: $\ast$target points to the beginning of the target buffer. Output\+: $\ast$target points to the first unit after the last char written. \\
\hline
{\em target\+Limit} & Pointer to the first unit after the target buffer. \\
\hline
{\em source} & I/O parameter, same as for \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afd107e398535c523d900f030df8326df}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+U\+Chars()}}. Input\+: $\ast$source points to the beginning of the source buffer. Output\+: $\ast$source points to the first unit after the last char read. \\
\hline
{\em source\+Limit} & Pointer to the first unit after the source buffer. \\
\hline
{\em pivot\+Start} & Pointer to the U\+T\+F-\/16 pivot buffer. If pivot\+Start==N\+U\+LL, then an internal buffer is used and the other pivot arguments are ignored and can be N\+U\+LL as well. \\
\hline
{\em pivot\+Source} & I/O parameter, same as source in \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a2cc3d9d8fbab664493a9aa189d120571}{ucnv\+\_\+from\+U\+Chars()}} for conversion from the pivot buffer to the target buffer. \\
\hline
{\em pivot\+Target} & I/O parameter, same as target in \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afd107e398535c523d900f030df8326df}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+U\+Chars()}} for conversion from the source buffer to the pivot buffer. It must be pivot\+Start$<$=$\ast$pivot\+Source$<$=$\ast$pivot\+Target$<$=pivot\+Limit and pivot\+Start$<$pivot\+Limit (unless pivot\+Start==N\+U\+LL). \\
\hline
{\em pivot\+Limit} & Pointer to the first unit after the pivot buffer. \\
\hline
{\em reset} & If true, then ucnv\+\_\+reset\+To\+Unicode(source\+Cnv) and ucnv\+\_\+reset\+From\+Unicode(target\+Cnv) are called, and the pivot pointers are reset ($\ast$pivot\+Target=$\ast$pivot\+Source=pivot\+Start). \\
\hline
{\em flush} & If true, indicates the end of the input. Passed directly to \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode()}}, and carried over to \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa63cf11835833041f2ce0ed3662edfcd}{ucnv\+\_\+from\+Unicode()}} when the source is empty as well. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & I\+CU error code in/out parameter. Must fulfill U\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS before the function call. U\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR always refers to the target buffer because overflows into the pivot buffer are handled internally. Other conversion errors are from the source-\/to-\/pivot conversion if $\ast$pivot\+Source==pivot\+Start, otherwise from the pivot-\/to-\/target conversion.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_countAliases()}{ucnv\_countAliases()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} uint16\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+count\+Aliases (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{alias,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Gives the number of aliases for a given converter or alias name. If the alias is ambiguous, then the preferred converter is used and the status is set to U\+\_\+\+A\+M\+B\+I\+G\+U\+O\+U\+S\+\_\+\+A\+L\+I\+A\+S\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG. This method only enumerates the listed entries in the alias file.

\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & error status \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a5be9c90442bc35a27ab42a4c0fbad5c3}\label{ucnv_8h_a5be9c90442bc35a27ab42a4c0fbad5c3}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_detectUnicodeSignature@{ucnv\_detectUnicodeSignature}}
\index{ucnv\_detectUnicodeSignature@{ucnv\_detectUnicodeSignature}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_detectUnicodeSignature()}{ucnv\_detectUnicodeSignature()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} char$\ast$ U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+detect\+Unicode\+Signature (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{source,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{source\+Length,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{signature\+Length,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Detects Unicode signature byte sequences at the start of the byte stream and returns the charset name of the indicated Unicode charset. N\+U\+LL is returned when no Unicode signature is recognized. The number of bytes in the signature is output as well.

The caller can \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a04af8743cca855974b87fd55a7970d6c}{ucnv\+\_\+open()}} a converter using the charset name. The first code unit (U\+Char) from the start of the stream will be U+\+F\+E\+FF (the Unicode B\+O\+M/signature character) and can usually be ignored.

For most Unicode charsets it is also possible to ignore the indicated number of initial stream bytes and start converting after them. However, there are stateful Unicode charsets (U\+T\+F-\/7 and B\+O\+C\+U-\/1) for which this will not work. Therefore, it is best to ignore the first output U\+Char instead of the input signature bytes. 

Usage\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}
\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em source} & The source string in which the signature should be detected. \\
\hline
{\em source\+Length} & Length of the input string, or -\/1 if terminated with a N\+UL byte. \\
\hline
{\em signature\+Length} & A pointer to int32\+\_\+t to receive the number of bytes that make up the signature of the detected U\+TF. 0 if not detected. Can be a N\+U\+LL pointer. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & I\+CU error code in/out parameter. Must fulfill U\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS before the function call. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The name of the encoding detected. N\+U\+LL if encoding is not detected. @stable I\+CU 2.\+4 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a5be456de4ae58f16325f99d097607473}\label{ucnv_8h_a5be456de4ae58f16325f99d097607473}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_fixFileSeparator@{ucnv\_fixFileSeparator}}
\index{ucnv\_fixFileSeparator@{ucnv\_fixFileSeparator}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_fixFileSeparator()}{ucnv\_fixFileSeparator()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+fix\+File\+Separator (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{cnv,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$}]{source,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{source\+Len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Fixes the backslash character mismapping. For example, in S\+J\+IS, the backslash character in the A\+S\+C\+II portion is also used to represent the yen currency sign. When mapping from Unicode character 0x005C, it\textquotesingle{}s unclear whether to map the character back to yen or backslash in S\+J\+IS. This function will take the input buffer and replace all the yen sign characters with backslash. This is necessary when the user tries to open a file with the input buffer on Windows. This function will test the converter to see whether such mapping is required. You can sometimes avoid using this function by using the correct version of Shift-\/\+J\+IS.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cnv} & The converter representing the target codepage. \\
\hline
{\em source} & the input buffer to be fixed \\
\hline
{\em source\+Len} & the length of the input buffer \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_ad809545cb8d0edf3067e1a5d690bf71f}{ucnv\+\_\+is\+Ambiguous}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+0 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a939c6148e6ebcf39568ce1c6ea0a24f0}\label{ucnv_8h_a939c6148e6ebcf39568ce1c6ea0a24f0}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_fromAlgorithmic@{ucnv\_fromAlgorithmic}}
\index{ucnv\_fromAlgorithmic@{ucnv\_fromAlgorithmic}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_fromAlgorithmic()}{ucnv\_fromAlgorithmic()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+from\+Algorithmic (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{cnv,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_adb0b44c6bd828c9d4cc2defcbba0f902}{U\+Converter\+Type}}}]{algorithmic\+Type,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{target,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{target\+Capacity,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{source,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{source\+Length,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Convert from one external charset to another. Internally, the text is converted to and from the 16-\/bit Unicode \char`\"{}pivot\char`\"{} using \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a1ab80dfe1f774537db9d5497a2ba8be7}{ucnv\+\_\+convert\+Ex()}}. \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a939c6148e6ebcf39568ce1c6ea0a24f0}{ucnv\+\_\+from\+Algorithmic()}} works exactly like \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a942e532c2f02bcaea39741d4b99764b5}{ucnv\+\_\+convert()}} except that the two converters need not be looked up and opened completely.

The source-\/to-\/pivot conversion uses a purely algorithmic converter according to the specified type, e.\+g., U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+U\+T\+F8 for a U\+T\+F-\/8 converter. The pivot-\/to-\/target conversion uses the cnv converter parameter.

Internally, the algorithmic converter is opened and closed for each function call, which is more efficient than using the public \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a04af8743cca855974b87fd55a7970d6c}{ucnv\+\_\+open()}} but somewhat less efficient than only resetting an existing converter and using \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a1ab80dfe1f774537db9d5497a2ba8be7}{ucnv\+\_\+convert\+Ex()}}.

This function is more convenient than \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a1ab80dfe1f774537db9d5497a2ba8be7}{ucnv\+\_\+convert\+Ex()}} for single-\/string conversions, especially when \char`\"{}preflighting\char`\"{} is desired (returning the length of the complete output even if it does not fit into the target buffer; see the User Guide Strings chapter). See \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a942e532c2f02bcaea39741d4b99764b5}{ucnv\+\_\+convert()}} for details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cnv} & The converter that is used to convert from the U\+T\+F-\/16 pivot buffer to the target. \\
\hline
{\em algorithmic\+Type} & U\+Converter\+Type constant identifying the desired source charset as a purely algorithmic converter. Those are converters for Unicode charsets like U\+T\+F-\/8, B\+O\+C\+U-\/1, S\+C\+SU, U\+T\+F-\/7, I\+M\+A\+P-\/mailbox-\/name, etc., as well as U\+S-\/\+A\+S\+C\+II and I\+S\+O-\/8859-\/1. \\
\hline
{\em target} & Pointer to the output buffer. \\
\hline
{\em target\+Capacity} & Capacity of the target, in bytes. \\
\hline
{\em source} & Pointer to the input buffer. \\
\hline
{\em source\+Length} & Length of the input text, in bytes \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & I\+CU error code in/out parameter. Must fulfill U\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS before the function call. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Length of the complete output text in bytes, even if it exceeds the target\+Capacity and a U\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR is set.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_fromUChars()}{ucnv\_fromUChars()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+from\+U\+Chars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{cnv,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{dest,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{dest\+Capacity,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{src\+Length,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Convert the Unicode string into a codepage string using an existing U\+Converter. The output string is N\+U\+L-\/terminated if possible.

This function is a more convenient but less powerful version of \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa63cf11835833041f2ce0ed3662edfcd}{ucnv\+\_\+from\+Unicode()}}. It is only useful for whole strings, not for streaming conversion.

The maximum output buffer capacity required (barring output from callbacks) will be \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa3d7e4ae84f8a95b9735ed3491cdb77e}{U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+T\+E\+S\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G(src\+Length, ucnv\+\_\+get\+Max\+Char\+Size(cnv))}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cnv} & the converter object to be used (\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aeb5938e9be0deb4a17575b073a98d37a}{ucnv\+\_\+reset\+From\+Unicode()}} will be called) \\
\hline
{\em src} & the input Unicode string \\
\hline
{\em src\+Length} & the input string length, or -\/1 if N\+U\+L-\/terminated \\
\hline
{\em dest} & destination string buffer, can be N\+U\+LL if dest\+Capacity==0 \\
\hline
{\em dest\+Capacity} & the number of chars available at dest \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & normal I\+CU error code; common error codes that may be set by this function include U\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR, U\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+R\+M\+I\+N\+A\+T\+E\+D\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG, U\+\_\+\+I\+L\+L\+E\+G\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR, and conversion errors \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the length of the output string, not counting the terminating N\+UL; if the length is greater than dest\+Capacity, then the string will not fit and a buffer of the indicated length would need to be passed in 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+from\+U\+Count\+Pending (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{cnv,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{status }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This function is useful for mapping semantics of I\+CU\textquotesingle{}s converter interface to those of iconv, and this information is not needed for normal conversion.

\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_fromUnicode@{ucnv\_fromUnicode}}
\index{ucnv\_fromUnicode@{ucnv\_fromUnicode}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_fromUnicode()}{ucnv\_fromUnicode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+from\+Unicode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{converter,  }\item[{char $\ast$$\ast$}]{target,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{target\+Limit,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$$\ast$}]{source,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$}]{source\+Limit,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{offsets,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}}}]{flush,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{err }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Converts an array of unicode characters to an array of codepage characters. This function is optimized for converting a continuous stream of data in buffer-\/sized chunks, where the entire source and target does not fit in available buffers.

The source pointer is an in/out parameter. It starts out pointing where the conversion is to begin, and ends up pointing after the last U\+Char consumed.

Target similarly starts out pointer at the first available byte in the output buffer, and ends up pointing after the last byte written to the output.

The converter always attempts to consume the entire source buffer, unless (1.) the target buffer is full, or (2.) a failing error is returned from the current callback function. When a successful error status has been returned, it means that all of the source buffer has been consumed. At that point, the caller should reset the source and source\+Limit pointers to point to the next chunk.

At the end of the stream (flush==true), the input is completely consumed when $\ast$source==source\+Limit and no error code is set. The converter object is then automatically reset by this function. (This means that a converter need not be reset explicitly between data streams if it finishes the previous stream without errors.)

This is a {\itshape stateful} conversion. Additionally, even when all source data has been consumed, some data may be in the converters\textquotesingle{} internal state. Call this function repeatedly, updating the target pointers with the next empty chunk of target in case of a {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR}, and updating the source pointers with the next chunk of source when a successful error status is returned, until there are no more chunks of source data. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em converter} & the Unicode converter \\
\hline
{\em target} & I/O parameter. Input \+: Points to the beginning of the buffer to copy codepage characters to. Output \+: points to after the last codepage character copied to {\ttfamily target}. \\
\hline
{\em target\+Limit} & the pointer just after last of the {\ttfamily target} buffer \\
\hline
{\em source} & I/O parameter, pointer to pointer to the source Unicode character buffer. \\
\hline
{\em source\+Limit} & the pointer just after the last of the source buffer \\
\hline
{\em offsets} & if N\+U\+LL is passed, nothing will happen to it, otherwise it needs to have the same number of allocated cells as {\ttfamily target}. Will fill in offsets from target to source pointer e.\+g\+: {\ttfamily offsets\mbox{[}3\mbox{]}} is equal to 6, it means that the {\ttfamily target\mbox{[}3\mbox{]}} was a result of transcoding {\ttfamily source\mbox{[}6\mbox{]}} For output data carried across calls, and other data without a specific source character (such as from escape sequences or callbacks) -\/1 will be placed for offsets. \\
\hline
{\em flush} & set to {\ttfamily true} if the current source buffer is the last available chunk of the source, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. Note that if a failing status is returned, this function may have to be called multiple times with flush set to {\ttfamily true} until the source buffer is consumed. \\
\hline
{\em err} & the error status. {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+I\+L\+L\+E\+G\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} will be set if the converter is {\ttfamily N\+U\+LL}. {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} will be set if the target is full and there is still data to be written to the target. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_getCanonicalName()}{ucnv\_getCanonicalName()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} char$\ast$ U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+get\+Canonical\+Name (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{alias,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{standard,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

 {\bfseries{\char`\"{}conv\char`\"{}}}

\index{ucnv\_getCCSID@{ucnv\_getCCSID}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_getCCSID()}{ucnv\_getCCSID()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+get\+C\+C\+S\+ID (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{converter,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{err }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Gets a codepage number associated with the converter. This is not guaranteed to be the one used to create the converter. Some converters do not represent platform registered codepages and return zero for the codepage number. The error code fill-\/in parameter indicates if the codepage number is available. Does not check if the converter is {\ttfamily N\+U\+LL} or if converter\textquotesingle{}s data table is {\ttfamily N\+U\+LL}.

Important\+: The use of C\+C\+S\+I\+Ds is not recommended because it is limited to only two platforms in principle and only one (U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+I\+BM) in the current I\+CU converter A\+PI. Also, C\+C\+S\+I\+Ds are insufficient to identify I\+BM Unicode conversion tables precisely. For more details see \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a3f54f96fcedd8d89f433c4bd9437864d}{ucnv\+\_\+open\+C\+C\+S\+I\+D()}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em converter} & the Unicode converter \\
\hline
{\em err} & the error status code. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
If any error occurs, -\/1 will be returned otherwise, the codepage number will be returned 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a3f54f96fcedd8d89f433c4bd9437864d}{ucnv\+\_\+open\+C\+C\+S\+ID}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a979fb8ddc407eccd2ac89d502d5245e5}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Platform}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+0

\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_ab284cb660babcd328f4e03f6f0b0b802}\label{ucnv_8h_ab284cb660babcd328f4e03f6f0b0b802}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_getMaxCharSize@{ucnv\_getMaxCharSize}}
\index{ucnv\_getMaxCharSize@{ucnv\_getMaxCharSize}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_getMaxCharSize()}{ucnv\_getMaxCharSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int8\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+get\+Max\+Char\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{converter }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the maximum number of bytes that are output per U\+Char in conversion from Unicode using this converter. The returned number can be used with U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+T\+E\+S\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+NG to calculate the size of a target buffer for conversion from Unicode.

Note\+: Before I\+CU 2.\+8, this function did not return reliable numbers for some stateful converters (E\+B\+C\+D\+I\+C\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+F\+UL, I\+S\+O-\/2022) and L\+M\+B\+CS.

This number may not be the same as the maximum number of bytes per \char`\"{}conversion unit\char`\"{}. In other words, it may not be the intuitively expected number of bytes per character that would be published for a charset, and may not fulfill any other purpose than the allocation of an output buffer of guaranteed sufficient size for a given input length and converter.

Examples for special cases that are taken into account\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Supplementary code points may convert to more bytes than B\+MP code points. This function returns bytes per U\+Char (U\+T\+F-\/16 code unit), not per Unicode code point, for efficient buffer allocation.
\item State-\/shifting output (S\+I/\+SO, escapes, etc.) from stateful converters.
\item When m input U\+Chars are converted to n output bytes, then the maximum m/n is taken into account.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The number returned here does not take into account (see U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+T\+E\+S\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+NG)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item callbacks which output more than one charset character sequence per call, like escape callbacks
\item initial and final non-\/character bytes that are output by some converters (automatic B\+O\+Ms, initial escape sequence, final SI, etc.)
\end{DoxyItemize}

Examples for returned values\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item S\+B\+CS charsets\+: 1
\item Shift-\/\+J\+IS\+: 2
\item U\+T\+F-\/16\+: 2 (2 per B\+MP, 4 per surrogate {\itshape pair}, B\+OM not counted)
\item U\+T\+F-\/8\+: 3 (3 per B\+MP, 4 per surrogate {\itshape pair})
\item E\+B\+C\+D\+I\+C\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+F\+UL (E\+B\+C\+D\+IC mixed S\+B\+C\+S/\+D\+B\+CS)\+: 3 (SO + D\+B\+CS)
\item I\+S\+O-\/2022\+: 3 (always outputs U\+T\+F-\/8)
\item I\+S\+O-\/2022-\/\+JP\+: 6 (4-\/byte escape sequences + D\+B\+CS)
\item I\+S\+O-\/2022-\/\+CN\+: 8 (4-\/byte designator sequences + 2-\/byte S\+S2/\+S\+S3 + D\+B\+CS)
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em converter} & The Unicode converter. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The maximum number of bytes per U\+Char (16 bit code unit) that are output by \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa63cf11835833041f2ce0ed3662edfcd}{ucnv\+\_\+from\+Unicode()}}, to be used together with U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+T\+E\+S\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+NG for buffer allocation.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa3d7e4ae84f8a95b9735ed3491cdb77e}{U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+T\+E\+S\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+NG}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a65f30417f0f0b249f449eb8d4e1100ce}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Min\+Char\+Size}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+0 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a65f30417f0f0b249f449eb8d4e1100ce}\label{ucnv_8h_a65f30417f0f0b249f449eb8d4e1100ce}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_getMinCharSize@{ucnv\_getMinCharSize}}
\index{ucnv\_getMinCharSize@{ucnv\_getMinCharSize}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_getMinCharSize()}{ucnv\_getMinCharSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int8\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+get\+Min\+Char\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{converter }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a032612b9d1f370e8831181c50b352dcf}\label{ucnv_8h_a032612b9d1f370e8831181c50b352dcf}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_getName@{ucnv\_getName}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily const \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} char$\ast$ U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+get\+Name (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{converter,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{err }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a00c0fdce8c98e50dea85beb3f086fe8e}\label{ucnv_8h_a00c0fdce8c98e50dea85beb3f086fe8e}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_getNextUChar@{ucnv\_getNextUChar}}
\index{ucnv\_getNextUChar@{ucnv\_getNextUChar}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_getNextUChar()}{ucnv\_getNextUChar()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+get\+Next\+U\+Char (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{converter,  }\item[{const char $\ast$$\ast$}]{source,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{source\+Limit,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{err }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Convert a codepage buffer into Unicode one character at a time. The input is completely consumed when the U\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+E\+X\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+O\+F\+B\+O\+U\+N\+D\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR is set.

Advantage compared to \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afd107e398535c523d900f030df8326df}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+U\+Chars()}}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Faster for small amounts of data, for most converters, e.\+g., U\+S-\/\+A\+S\+C\+II, I\+S\+O-\/8859-\/1, U\+T\+F-\/8/16/32, and most \char`\"{}normal\char`\"{} charsets. (For complex converters, e.\+g., S\+C\+SU, U\+T\+F-\/7 and I\+SO 2022 variants, it uses \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode()}} internally.)
\item Convenient.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Limitations compared to \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode()}}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Always assumes flush=true. This makes \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a00c0fdce8c98e50dea85beb3f086fe8e}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Next\+U\+Char()}} unsuitable for \char`\"{}streaming\char`\"{} conversion, that is, for where the input is supplied in multiple buffers, because \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a00c0fdce8c98e50dea85beb3f086fe8e}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Next\+U\+Char()}} will assume the end of the input at the end of the first buffer.
\item Does not provide offset output.
\end{DoxyItemize}

It is possible to \char`\"{}mix\char`\"{} \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a00c0fdce8c98e50dea85beb3f086fe8e}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Next\+U\+Char()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode()}} because \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a00c0fdce8c98e50dea85beb3f086fe8e}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Next\+U\+Char()}} uses the current state of the converter (unlike \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afd107e398535c523d900f030df8326df}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+U\+Chars()}} which always resets first). However, if \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a00c0fdce8c98e50dea85beb3f086fe8e}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Next\+U\+Char()}} is called after \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode()}} stopped in the middle of a character sequence (with flush=false), then \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a00c0fdce8c98e50dea85beb3f086fe8e}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Next\+U\+Char()}} will always use the slower \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode()}} internally until the next character boundary. (This is new in I\+CU 2.\+6. In earlier releases, \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a00c0fdce8c98e50dea85beb3f086fe8e}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Next\+U\+Char()}} had to start at a character boundary.)

Instead of using \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a00c0fdce8c98e50dea85beb3f086fe8e}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Next\+U\+Char()}}, it is recommended to convert using \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afd107e398535c523d900f030df8326df}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+U\+Chars()}} and then iterate over the text using \mbox{\hyperlink{utf16_8h_a844bb48486904fdca40c8b883e9c80ee}{U16\+\_\+\+N\+E\+X\+T()}} or a \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_char_iterator}{U\+Char\+Iterator}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{uiter_8h}{uiter.\+h}}) or a C++ Character\+Iterator or similar. This allows streaming conversion and offset output, for example.

Handling of surrogate pairs and supplementary-\/plane code points\+:~\newline
 There are two different kinds of codepages that provide mappings for surrogate characters\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Codepages like U\+T\+F-\/8, U\+T\+F-\/32, and GB 18030 provide direct representations for Unicode code points U+10000-\/\+U+10ffff as well as for single surrogates U+d800-\/\+U+dfff. Each valid sequence will result in exactly one returned code point. If a sequence results in a single surrogate, then that will be returned by itself, even if a neighboring sequence encodes the matching surrogate. 
\item Codepages like S\+C\+SU and L\+M\+B\+CS (and U\+T\+F-\/16) provide direct representations only for B\+MP code points including surrogates. Code points in supplementary planes are represented with two sequences, each encoding a surrogate. For these codepages, matching pairs of surrogates will be combined into single code points for returning from this function. (Note that S\+C\+SU is actually a mix of these codepage types.) 
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em converter} & an open U\+Converter \\
\hline
{\em source} & the address of a pointer to the codepage buffer, will be updated to point after the bytes consumed in the conversion call. \\
\hline
{\em source\+Limit} & points to the end of the input buffer \\
\hline
{\em err} & fills in error status (see ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode) {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+E\+X\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+O\+F\+B\+O\+U\+N\+D\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} will be set if the input is empty or does not convert to any output (e.\+g.\+: pure state-\/change codes S\+I/\+SO, escape sequences for I\+SO 2022, or if the callback did not output anything, ...). This function will not set a {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} because the \char`\"{}buffer\char`\"{} is the return code. However, there might be subsequent output stored in the converter object that will be returned in following calls to this function. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a U\+Char32 resulting from the partial conversion of source 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Gets the \char`\"{}starter\char`\"{} (lead) bytes for converters of type M\+B\+CS. Will fill in an {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+I\+L\+L\+E\+G\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} if converter passed in is not M\+B\+CS. Fills in an array of type U\+Bool, with the value of the byte as offset to the array. For example, if (starters\mbox{[}0x20\mbox{]} == true) at return, it means that the byte 0x20 is a starter byte in this converter. Context pointers are always owned by the caller.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_getUnicodeSet()}{ucnv\_getUnicodeSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+get\+Unicode\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{cnv,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_adce3fef7c15d7c78196bf977ac96ec9c}{U\+Set}} $\ast$}]{set\+Fill\+In,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a402221896b6d7153b14a5ff8dadde806}{U\+Converter\+Unicode\+Set}}}]{which\+Set,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the set of Unicode code points that can be converted by an I\+CU converter.

Returns one of several kinds of set\+:


\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+T\+R\+I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+ET
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

The set of all Unicode code points that can be roundtrip-\/converted (converted without any data loss) with the converter (\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa63cf11835833041f2ce0ed3662edfcd}{ucnv\+\_\+from\+Unicode()}}). This set will not include code points that have fallback mappings or are only the result of reverse fallback mappings. This set will also not include P\+UA code points with fallbacks, although \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa63cf11835833041f2ce0ed3662edfcd}{ucnv\+\_\+from\+Unicode()}} will always uses those mappings despite \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a6a1f70909aa917783b1ec6f350bde107}{ucnv\+\_\+set\+Fallback()}}. See U\+TR \#22 \char`\"{}\+Character Mapping Markup Language\char`\"{} at \href{http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr22/}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+unicode.\+org/reports/tr22/}}

This is useful for example for
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item checking that a string or document can be roundtrip-\/converted with a converter, without/before actually performing the conversion
\item testing if a converter can be used for text for typical text for a certain locale, by comparing its roundtrip set with the set of Exemplar\+Characters from I\+CU\textquotesingle{}s locale data or other sources
\end{DoxyItemize}
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+T\+R\+I\+P\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+S\+ET
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

The set of all Unicode code points that can be converted with the converter (\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa63cf11835833041f2ce0ed3662edfcd}{ucnv\+\_\+from\+Unicode()}}) when fallbacks are turned on (see \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a6a1f70909aa917783b1ec6f350bde107}{ucnv\+\_\+set\+Fallback()}}). This set includes all code points with roundtrips and fallbacks (but not reverse fallbacks).

In the future, there may be more U\+Converter\+Unicode\+Set choices to select sets with different properties.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cnv} & The converter for which a set is requested. \\
\hline
{\em set\+Fill\+In} & A valid U\+Set $\ast$. It will be cleared by this function before the converter\textquotesingle{}s specific set is filled into the U\+Set. \\
\hline
{\em which\+Set} & A U\+Converter\+Unicode\+Set selector; currently U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+T\+R\+I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+ET is the only supported value. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & I\+CU error code in/out parameter. Must fulfill U\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS before the function call.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a402221896b6d7153b14a5ff8dadde806}{U\+Converter\+Unicode\+Set}}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_isFixedWidth@{ucnv\_isFixedWidth}}
\index{ucnv\_isFixedWidth@{ucnv\_isFixedWidth}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_isFixedWidth()}{ucnv\_isFixedWidth()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+is\+Fixed\+Width (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{cnv,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{status }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns whether or not the charset of the converter has a fixed number of bytes per charset character. An example of this are converters that are of the type U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+S\+B\+CS or U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+D\+B\+CS. Another example is U\+T\+F-\/32 which is always 4 bytes per character. A Unicode code point may be represented by more than one U\+T\+F-\/8 or U\+T\+F-\/16 code unit but a U\+T\+F-\/32 converter encodes each code point with 4 bytes. Note\+: This method is not intended to be used to determine whether the charset has a fixed ratio of bytes to Unicode codes {\itshape units} for any particular Unicode encoding form. false is returned with the U\+Error\+Code if error occurs or cnv is N\+U\+LL. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cnv} & The converter to be tested \\
\hline
{\em status} & I\+CU error code in/out paramter \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the converter is fixed-\/width @stable I\+CU 4.\+8 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a04af8743cca855974b87fd55a7970d6c}\label{ucnv_8h_a04af8743cca855974b87fd55a7970d6c}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_open@{ucnv\_open}}
\index{ucnv\_open@{ucnv\_open}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_open()}{ucnv\_open()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}}$\ast$ U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+open (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{converter\+Name,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{err }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a U\+Converter object with the name of a coded character set specified as a C string. The actual name will be resolved with the alias file using a case-\/insensitive string comparison that ignores leading zeroes and all non-\/alphanumeric characters. E.\+g., the names \char`\"{}\+U\+T\+F8\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}utf-\/8\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}u$\ast$\+T@f08\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}\+Utf 8\char`\"{} are all equivalent. (See also \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a8d23f178a9474210cce08530fbfe6ab3}{ucnv\+\_\+compare\+Names()}}.) If {\ttfamily N\+U\+LL} is passed for the converter name, it will create one with the get\+Default\+Name return value.

A converter name for I\+CU 1.\+5 and above may contain options like a locale specification to control the specific behavior of the newly instantiated converter. The meaning of the options depends on the particular converter. If an option is not defined for or recognized by a given converter, then it is ignored.

Options are appended to the converter name string, with a {\ttfamily U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+E\+P\+\_\+\+C\+H\+AR} between the name and the first option and also between adjacent options.

If the alias is ambiguous, then the preferred converter is used and the status is set to U\+\_\+\+A\+M\+B\+I\+G\+U\+O\+U\+S\+\_\+\+A\+L\+I\+A\+S\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG.

The conversion behavior and names can vary between platforms. I\+CU may convert some characters differently from other platforms. Details on this topic are in the \href{http://icu-project.org/userguide/conversion.html}{\texttt{ User\textquotesingle{}s Guide}}. Aliases starting with a \char`\"{}cp\char`\"{} prefix have no specific meaning other than its an alias starting with the letters \char`\"{}cp\char`\"{}. Please do not associate any meaning to these aliases.


\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}
\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em converter\+Name} & Name of the coded character set table. This may have options appended to the string. I\+A\+NA alias character set names, I\+BM C\+C\+S\+I\+Ds starting with \char`\"{}ibm-\/\char`\"{}, Windows codepage numbers starting with \char`\"{}windows-\/\char`\"{} are frequently used for this parameter. See ucnv\+\_\+get\+Available\+Name and ucnv\+\_\+get\+Alias for a complete list that is available. If this parameter is N\+U\+LL, the default converter will be used. \\
\hline
{\em err} & outgoing error status {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR, U\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the created Unicode converter object, or {\ttfamily N\+U\+LL} if an error occurred 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a2bc7b6cbf949eaed1814d3c28b1eb3cf}\label{ucnv_8h_a2bc7b6cbf949eaed1814d3c28b1eb3cf}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_openAllNames@{ucnv\_openAllNames}}
\index{ucnv\_openAllNames@{ucnv\_openAllNames}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_openAllNames()}{ucnv\_openAllNames()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{uenum_8h_a32b7253b2148022535be36a9fcdb5a8d}{U\+Enumeration}}$\ast$ U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+open\+All\+Names (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

A U\+Enumeration object for getting all the recognized canonical converter names.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a3f54f96fcedd8d89f433c4bd9437864d}\label{ucnv_8h_a3f54f96fcedd8d89f433c4bd9437864d}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_openCCSID@{ucnv\_openCCSID}}
\index{ucnv\_openCCSID@{ucnv\_openCCSID}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_openCCSID()}{ucnv\_openCCSID()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}}$\ast$ U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+open\+C\+C\+S\+ID (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{codepage,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aba5ba7fbc2f113618ba57f4d9825ff85}{U\+Converter\+Platform}}}]{platform,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{err }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a U\+Converter object from a C\+C\+S\+ID number and platform pair. Note that the usefulness of this function is limited to platforms with numeric encoding I\+Ds. Only I\+BM and Microsoft platforms use numeric (16-\/bit) identifiers for encodings.

In addition, I\+BM C\+C\+S\+I\+Ds and Unicode conversion tables are not 1\+:1 related. For many I\+BM C\+C\+S\+I\+Ds there are multiple (up to six) Unicode conversion tables, and for some Unicode conversion tables there are multiple C\+C\+S\+I\+Ds. Some \char`\"{}alternate\char`\"{} Unicode conversion tables are provided by the I\+BM C\+D\+RA conversion table registry. The most prominent example of a systematic modification of conversion tables that is not provided in the form of conversion table files in the repository is that S/390 Unix System Services swaps the codes for Line Feed and New Line in all E\+B\+C\+D\+IC codepages, which requires such a swap in the Unicode conversion tables as well.

Only I\+BM default conversion tables are accessible with \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a3f54f96fcedd8d89f433c4bd9437864d}{ucnv\+\_\+open\+C\+C\+S\+I\+D()}}. \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_ad17df5c1434e7f5fd3c2871543428346}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+C\+C\+S\+I\+D()}} will return the same C\+C\+S\+ID for all conversion tables that are associated with that C\+C\+S\+ID.

Currently, the only \char`\"{}platform\char`\"{} supported in the I\+CU converter A\+PI is U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+I\+BM.

In summary, the use of C\+C\+S\+I\+Ds and the associated A\+PI functions is not recommended.

In order to open a converter with the default I\+BM C\+D\+RA Unicode conversion table, you can use this function or use the prefix \char`\"{}ibm-\/\char`\"{}\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{char} name[20];}
\DoxyCodeLine{sprintf(name, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"ibm-\/\%hu"}, ccsid);}
\DoxyCodeLine{cnv=\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a04af8743cca855974b87fd55a7970d6c}{ucnv\_open}}(name, \&errorCode);}
\end{DoxyCode}


In order to open a converter with the I\+BM S/390 Unix System Services variant of a Unicode/\+E\+B\+C\+D\+IC conversion table, you can use the prefix \char`\"{}ibm-\/\char`\"{} together with the option string U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+S\+W\+A\+P\+\_\+\+L\+F\+N\+L\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+NG\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{char} name[20];}
\DoxyCodeLine{sprintf(name, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"ibm-\/\%hu"} \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a0588f7014923ad969821941f9dd51040}{UCNV\_SWAP\_LFNL\_OPTION\_STRING}}, ccsid);}
\DoxyCodeLine{cnv=\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a04af8743cca855974b87fd55a7970d6c}{ucnv\_open}}(name, \&errorCode);}
\end{DoxyCode}


In order to open a converter from a Microsoft codepage number, use the prefix \char`\"{}cp\char`\"{}\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{char} name[20];}
\DoxyCodeLine{sprintf(name, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"cp\%hu"}, codepageID);}
\DoxyCodeLine{cnv=\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a04af8743cca855974b87fd55a7970d6c}{ucnv\_open}}(name, \&errorCode);}
\end{DoxyCode}


If the alias is ambiguous, then the preferred converter is used and the status is set to U\+\_\+\+A\+M\+B\+I\+G\+U\+O\+U\+S\+\_\+\+A\+L\+I\+A\+S\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em codepage} & codepage number to create \\
\hline
{\em platform} & the platform in which the codepage number exists \\
\hline
{\em err} & error status {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR, U\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the created Unicode converter object, or {\ttfamily N\+U\+LL} if an error occurred. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a04af8743cca855974b87fd55a7970d6c}{ucnv\+\_\+open}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_ad3f473f991769a94f21e195473470157}{ucnv\+\_\+openU}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a499316e130bdd073c394c92f55c315d2}{ucnv\+\_\+close}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_openPackage()}{ucnv\_openPackage()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}}$\ast$ U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+open\+Package (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{package\+Name,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{converter\+Name,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{err }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a U\+Converter object specified from a package\+Name and a converter\+Name.

The package\+Name and converter\+Name must point to an I\+CU udata object, as defined by {\ttfamily  udata\+\_\+open( package\+Name, \char`\"{}cnv\char`\"{}, converter\+Name, err) } or equivalent. Typically, package\+Name will refer to a (.dat) file, or to a package registered with \mbox{\hyperlink{udata_8h_a8a44e57ac1388440e90c58d606df9b90}{udata\+\_\+set\+App\+Data()}}. Using a full file or directory pathname for package\+Name is deprecated.

The name will N\+OT be looked up in the alias mechanism, nor will the converter be stored in the converter cache or the alias table. The only way to open further converters is call this function multiple times, or use the \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aebb51e41917fe9b0488cfdb5717ff826}{ucnv\+\_\+safe\+Clone()}} function to clone a \textquotesingle{}primary\textquotesingle{} converter.

A future version of I\+CU may add alias table lookups and/or caching to this function.

Example Use\+: {\ttfamily cnv = ucnv\+\_\+open\+Package(\char`\"{}myapp\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}myconverter\char`\"{}, \&err);} 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em package\+Name} & name of the package (equivalent to \textquotesingle{}path\textquotesingle{} in \mbox{\hyperlink{udata_8h_aa665f05301670184392e3ceb8dd149fb}{udata\+\_\+open()}} call) \\
\hline
{\em converter\+Name} & name of the data item to be used, without suffix. \\
\hline
{\em err} & outgoing error status {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR, U\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the created Unicode converter object, or {\ttfamily N\+U\+LL} if an error occurred 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{udata_8h_aa665f05301670184392e3ceb8dd149fb}{udata\+\_\+open}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_openStandardNames()}{ucnv\_openStandardNames()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{uenum_8h_a32b7253b2148022535be36a9fcdb5a8d}{U\+Enumeration}}$\ast$ U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+open\+Standard\+Names (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{conv\+Name,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{standard,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Return a new U\+Enumeration object for enumerating all the alias names for a given converter that are recognized by a standard. This method only enumerates the listed entries in the alias file. The convrtrs.\+txt file can be modified to change the results of this function. The first result in this list is the same result given by {\ttfamily ucnv\+\_\+get\+Standard\+Name}, which is the default alias for the specified standard name. The returned object must be closed with {\ttfamily uenum\+\_\+close} when you are done with the object.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conv\+Name} & original converter name \\
\hline
{\em standard} & name of the standard governing the names; M\+I\+ME and I\+A\+NA are such standards \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & The error code \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A U\+Enumeration object for getting all aliases that are recognized by a standard. If any of the parameters are invalid, N\+U\+LL is returned. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_ab713bdfeeea22684aa5bbbf2e00d23ef}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Standard\+Name}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_openU()}{ucnv\_openU()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}}$\ast$ U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+openU (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$}]{name,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{err }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a Unicode converter with the names specified as unicode string. The name should be limited to the A\+S\+C\+I\+I-\/7 alphanumerics range. The actual name will be resolved with the alias file using a case-\/insensitive string comparison that ignores leading zeroes and all non-\/alphanumeric characters. E.\+g., the names \char`\"{}\+U\+T\+F8\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}utf-\/8\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}u$\ast$\+T@f08\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}\+Utf 8\char`\"{} are all equivalent. (See also \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a8d23f178a9474210cce08530fbfe6ab3}{ucnv\+\_\+compare\+Names()}}.) If {\ttfamily N\+U\+LL} is passed for the converter name, it will create one with the \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a34a9f2aae7fb71436cab7ace6945d35d}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Default\+Name()}} return value. If the alias is ambiguous, then the preferred converter is used and the status is set to U\+\_\+\+A\+M\+B\+I\+G\+U\+O\+U\+S\+\_\+\+A\+L\+I\+A\+S\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG.

See ucnv\+\_\+open for the complete details


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em name} & Name of the U\+Converter table in a zero terminated Unicode string \\
\hline
{\em err} & outgoing error status {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR, U\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the created Unicode converter object, or {\ttfamily N\+U\+LL} if an error occurred 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_safeClone@{ucnv\_safeClone}}
\index{ucnv\_safeClone@{ucnv\_safeClone}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_safeClone()}{ucnv\_safeClone()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}}$\ast$ U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+safe\+Clone (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{cnv,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{stack\+Buffer,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{p\+Buffer\+Size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{status }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Thread safe converter cloning operation. For most efficient operation, pass in a stack\+Buffer (and a $\ast$p\+Buffer\+Size) with at least U\+\_\+\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+S\+A\+F\+E\+C\+L\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ZE bytes of space. If the buffer size is sufficient, then the clone will use the stack buffer; otherwise, it will be allocated, and $\ast$p\+Buffer\+Size will indicate the actual size. (This should not occur with U\+\_\+\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+S\+A\+F\+E\+C\+L\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ZE.)

You must \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a499316e130bdd073c394c92f55c315d2}{ucnv\+\_\+close()}} the clone in any case.

If $\ast$p\+Buffer\+Size==0, (regardless of whether stack\+Buffer==N\+U\+LL or not) then $\ast$p\+Buffer\+Size will be changed to a sufficient size for cloning this converter, without actually cloning the converter (\char`\"{}pure pre-\/flighting\char`\"{}).

If $\ast$p\+Buffer\+Size is greater than zero but not large enough for a stack-\/based clone, then the converter is cloned using newly allocated memory and $\ast$p\+Buffer\+Size is changed to the necessary size.

If the converter clone fits into the stack buffer but the stack buffer is not sufficiently aligned for the clone, then the clone will use an adjusted pointer and use an accordingly smaller buffer size.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cnv} & converter to be cloned \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Buffer} & {\itshape Deprecated functionality as of I\+CU 52, use N\+U\+LL.}~\newline
 user allocated space for the new clone. If N\+U\+LL new memory will be allocated. If buffer is not large enough, new memory will be allocated. Clients can use the U\+\_\+\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+S\+A\+F\+E\+C\+L\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ZE. This will probably be enough to avoid memory allocations. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Buffer\+Size} & {\itshape Deprecated functionality as of I\+CU 52, use N\+U\+LL or 1.}~\newline
 pointer to size of allocated space. \\
\hline
{\em status} & to indicate whether the operation went on smoothly or there were errors An informational status value, U\+\_\+\+S\+A\+F\+E\+C\+L\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+D\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG, is used if any allocations were necessary. However, it is better to check if $\ast$p\+Buffer\+Size grew for checking for allocations because warning codes can be overridden by subsequent function calls. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
pointer to the new clone @stable I\+CU 2.\+0 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a8a983781f10d4e1e7f19ca2e1c6a4de9}\label{ucnv_8h_a8a983781f10d4e1e7f19ca2e1c6a4de9}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_setDefaultName()}{ucnv\_setDefaultName()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+set\+Default\+Name (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{name }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This function is not thread safe. DO N\+OT call this function when A\+NY I\+CU function is being used from more than one thread! This function sets the current default converter name. If this function needs to be called, it should be called during application initialization. Most of the time, the results from \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a34a9f2aae7fb71436cab7ace6945d35d}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Default\+Name()}} or ucnv\+\_\+open with a N\+U\+LL string argument is sufficient for your application.

If U\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+R\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+U\+T\+F8 is defined to 1 in \mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h}{utypes.\+h}} then this function does nothing.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+set\+Fallback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{cnv,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}}}]{uses\+Fallback }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the converter to use fallback mappings or not. Regardless of this flag, the converter will always use fallbacks from Unicode Private Use code points, as well as reverse fallbacks (to Unicode). For details see \char`\"{}.\+ucm File Format\char`\"{} in the Conversion Data chapter of the I\+CU User Guide\+: \href{http://www.icu-project.org/userguide/conversion-data.html\#ucmformat}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+icu-\/project.\+org/userguide/conversion-\/data.\+html\#ucmformat}}
