\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_setSubstChars@{ucnv\_setSubstChars}}
\index{ucnv\_setSubstChars@{ucnv\_setSubstChars}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_setSubstChars()}{ucnv\_setSubstChars()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+set\+Subst\+Chars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{converter,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{sub\+Chars,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{len,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{err }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the substitution chars when converting from unicode to a codepage. The substitution is specified as a string of 1-\/4 bytes, and may contain {\ttfamily N\+U\+LL} bytes. The sub\+Chars must represent a single character. The caller needs to know the byte sequence of a valid character in the converter\textquotesingle{}s charset. For some converters, for example some I\+SO 2022 variants, only single-\/byte substitution characters may be supported. The newer \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a38e2e21ab52bd6fab1c4cb21d00fd23f}{ucnv\+\_\+set\+Subst\+String()}} function relaxes these limitations.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em converter} & the Unicode converter \\
\hline
{\em sub\+Chars} & the substitution character byte sequence we want set \\
\hline
{\em len} & the number of bytes in sub\+Chars \\
\hline
{\em err} & the error status code. {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+E\+X\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+O\+F\+B\+O\+U\+N\+D\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR } if len is bigger than the maximum number of bytes allowed in subchars \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a38e2e21ab52bd6fab1c4cb21d00fd23f}{ucnv\+\_\+set\+Subst\+String}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a8a670af025c7632628b450daa50e47df}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Subst\+Chars}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+0 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a38e2e21ab52bd6fab1c4cb21d00fd23f}\label{ucnv_8h_a38e2e21ab52bd6fab1c4cb21d00fd23f}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_setSubstString@{ucnv\_setSubstString}}
\index{ucnv\_setSubstString@{ucnv\_setSubstString}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_setSubstString()}{ucnv\_setSubstString()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+set\+Subst\+String (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{cnv,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$}]{s,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{length,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{err }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set a substitution string for converting from Unicode to a charset. The caller need not know the charset byte sequence for each charset.

Unlike \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa840af123bebe51ecdb936641087f229}{ucnv\+\_\+set\+Subst\+Chars()}} which is designed to set a charset byte sequence for a single character, this function takes a Unicode string with zero, one or more characters, and immediately verifies that the string can be converted to the charset. If not, or if the result is too long (more than 32 bytes as of I\+CU 3.\+6), then the function returns with an error accordingly.

Also unlike \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa840af123bebe51ecdb936641087f229}{ucnv\+\_\+set\+Subst\+Chars()}}, this function works for stateful charsets by converting on the fly at the point of substitution rather than setting a fixed byte sequence.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cnv} & The U\+Converter object. \\
\hline
{\em s} & The Unicode string. \\
\hline
{\em length} & The number of U\+Chars in s, or -\/1 for a N\+U\+L-\/terminated string. \\
\hline
{\em err} & Pointer to a standard I\+CU error code. Its input value must pass the \mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a527f2c69e6b2e3b2c53ad8a99fb36711}{U\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+S\+S()}} test, or else the function returns immediately. Check for \mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a4d202200b6aa6f3c965ea370e0c8155f}{U\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+R\+E()}} on output or use with function chaining. (See User Guide for details.)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aa840af123bebe51ecdb936641087f229}{ucnv\+\_\+set\+Subst\+Chars}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a8a670af025c7632628b450daa50e47df}{ucnv\+\_\+get\+Subst\+Chars}} @stable I\+CU 3.\+6 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+set\+To\+U\+Call\+Back (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{converter,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_ae077d9f2a37d3aa640c3c2032a2baa2c}{U\+Converter\+To\+U\+Callback}}}]{new\+Action,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{new\+Context,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_ae077d9f2a37d3aa640c3c2032a2baa2c}{U\+Converter\+To\+U\+Callback}} $\ast$}]{old\+Action,  }\item[{const void $\ast$$\ast$}]{old\+Context,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{err }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_a872d74b772834c4c7924edfe1f933691}\label{ucnv_8h_a872d74b772834c4c7924edfe1f933691}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_toAlgorithmic@{ucnv\_toAlgorithmic}}
\index{ucnv\_toAlgorithmic@{ucnv\_toAlgorithmic}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_toAlgorithmic()}{ucnv\_toAlgorithmic()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+to\+Algorithmic (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_adb0b44c6bd828c9d4cc2defcbba0f902}{U\+Converter\+Type}}}]{algorithmic\+Type,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{cnv,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{target,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{target\+Capacity,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{source,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{source\+Length,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Convert from one external charset to another. Internally, the text is converted to and from the 16-\/bit Unicode \char`\"{}pivot\char`\"{} using \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a1ab80dfe1f774537db9d5497a2ba8be7}{ucnv\+\_\+convert\+Ex()}}. \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a872d74b772834c4c7924edfe1f933691}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+Algorithmic()}} works exactly like \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a942e532c2f02bcaea39741d4b99764b5}{ucnv\+\_\+convert()}} except that the two converters need not be looked up and opened completely.

The source-\/to-\/pivot conversion uses the cnv converter parameter. The pivot-\/to-\/target conversion uses a purely algorithmic converter according to the specified type, e.\+g., U\+C\+N\+V\+\_\+\+U\+T\+F8 for a U\+T\+F-\/8 converter.

Internally, the algorithmic converter is opened and closed for each function call, which is more efficient than using the public \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a04af8743cca855974b87fd55a7970d6c}{ucnv\+\_\+open()}} but somewhat less efficient than only resetting an existing converter and using \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a1ab80dfe1f774537db9d5497a2ba8be7}{ucnv\+\_\+convert\+Ex()}}.

This function is more convenient than \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a1ab80dfe1f774537db9d5497a2ba8be7}{ucnv\+\_\+convert\+Ex()}} for single-\/string conversions, especially when \char`\"{}preflighting\char`\"{} is desired (returning the length of the complete output even if it does not fit into the target buffer; see the User Guide Strings chapter). See \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_a942e532c2f02bcaea39741d4b99764b5}{ucnv\+\_\+convert()}} for details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em algorithmic\+Type} & U\+Converter\+Type constant identifying the desired target charset as a purely algorithmic converter. Those are converters for Unicode charsets like U\+T\+F-\/8, B\+O\+C\+U-\/1, S\+C\+SU, U\+T\+F-\/7, I\+M\+A\+P-\/mailbox-\/name, etc., as well as U\+S-\/\+A\+S\+C\+II and I\+S\+O-\/8859-\/1. \\
\hline
{\em cnv} & The converter that is used to convert from the source to the U\+T\+F-\/16 pivot buffer. \\
\hline
{\em target} & Pointer to the output buffer. \\
\hline
{\em target\+Capacity} & Capacity of the target, in bytes. \\
\hline
{\em source} & Pointer to the input buffer. \\
\hline
{\em source\+Length} & Length of the input text, in bytes \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & I\+CU error code in/out parameter. Must fulfill U\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS before the function call. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Length of the complete output text in bytes, even if it exceeds the target\+Capacity and a U\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR is set.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_toUChars()}{ucnv\_toUChars()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+to\+U\+Chars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{cnv,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$}]{dest,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{dest\+Capacity,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{src\+Length,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Convert the codepage string into a Unicode string using an existing U\+Converter. The output string is N\+U\+L-\/terminated if possible.

This function is a more convenient but less powerful version of \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}{ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode()}}. It is only useful for whole strings, not for streaming conversion.

The maximum output buffer capacity required (barring output from callbacks) will be 2$\ast$src\+Length (each char may be converted into a surrogate pair).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cnv} & the converter object to be used (\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv_8h_aedbb912ce9067a392052bc91a7d9ee34}{ucnv\+\_\+reset\+To\+Unicode()}} will be called) \\
\hline
{\em src} & the input codepage string \\
\hline
{\em src\+Length} & the input string length, or -\/1 if N\+U\+L-\/terminated \\
\hline
{\em dest} & destination string buffer, can be N\+U\+LL if dest\+Capacity==0 \\
\hline
{\em dest\+Capacity} & the number of U\+Chars available at dest \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & normal I\+CU error code; common error codes that may be set by this function include U\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR, U\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+R\+M\+I\+N\+A\+T\+E\+D\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG, U\+\_\+\+I\+L\+L\+E\+G\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR, and conversion errors \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the length of the output string, not counting the terminating N\+UL; if the length is greater than dest\+Capacity, then the string will not fit and a buffer of the indicated length would need to be passed in 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_toUCountPending()}{ucnv\_toUCountPending()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+to\+U\+Count\+Pending (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{cnv,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{status }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the number of chars held in the converter\textquotesingle{}s internal state because more input is needed for completing the conversion. This function is useful for mapping semantics of I\+CU\textquotesingle{}s converter interface to those of iconv, and this information is not needed for normal conversion.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}\label{ucnv_8h_afbbface3193728333668691daaf2fbfb}} 
\index{ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}!ucnv\_toUnicode@{ucnv\_toUnicode}}
\index{ucnv\_toUnicode@{ucnv\_toUnicode}!ucnv.h@{ucnv.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_toUnicode()}{ucnv\_toUnicode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+to\+Unicode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{converter,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$$\ast$}]{target,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a6bb9fad572d65b305324ef288165e2ac}{U\+Char}} $\ast$}]{target\+Limit,  }\item[{const char $\ast$$\ast$}]{source,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{source\+Limit,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{offsets,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}}}]{flush,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{err }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Converts a buffer of codepage bytes into an array of unicode U\+Chars characters. This function is optimized for converting a continuous stream of data in buffer-\/sized chunks, where the entire source and target does not fit in available buffers.

The source pointer is an in/out parameter. It starts out pointing where the conversion is to begin, and ends up pointing after the last byte of source consumed.

Target similarly starts out pointer at the first available U\+Char in the output buffer, and ends up pointing after the last U\+Char written to the output. It does N\+OT necessarily keep U\+Char sequences together.

The converter always attempts to consume the entire source buffer, unless (1.) the target buffer is full, or (2.) a failing error is returned from the current callback function. When a successful error status has been returned, it means that all of the source buffer has been consumed. At that point, the caller should reset the source and source\+Limit pointers to point to the next chunk.

At the end of the stream (flush==true), the input is completely consumed when $\ast$source==source\+Limit and no error code is set The converter object is then automatically reset by this function. (This means that a converter need not be reset explicitly between data streams if it finishes the previous stream without errors.)

This is a {\itshape stateful} conversion. Additionally, even when all source data has been consumed, some data may be in the converters\textquotesingle{} internal state. Call this function repeatedly, updating the target pointers with the next empty chunk of target in case of a {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR}, and updating the source pointers with the next chunk of source when a successful error status is returned, until there are no more chunks of source data. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em converter} & the Unicode converter \\
\hline
{\em target} & I/O parameter. Input \+: Points to the beginning of the buffer to copy U\+Chars into. Output \+: points to after the last U\+Char copied. \\
\hline
{\em target\+Limit} & the pointer just after the end of the {\ttfamily target} buffer \\
\hline
{\em source} & I/O parameter, pointer to pointer to the source codepage buffer. \\
\hline
{\em source\+Limit} & the pointer to the byte after the end of the source buffer \\
\hline
{\em offsets} & if N\+U\+LL is passed, nothing will happen to it, otherwise it needs to have the same number of allocated cells as {\ttfamily target}. Will fill in offsets from target to source pointer e.\+g\+: {\ttfamily offsets\mbox{[}3\mbox{]}} is equal to 6, it means that the {\ttfamily target\mbox{[}3\mbox{]}} was a result of transcoding {\ttfamily source\mbox{[}6\mbox{]}} For output data carried across calls, and other data without a specific source character (such as from escape sequences or callbacks) -\/1 will be placed for offsets. \\
\hline
{\em flush} & set to {\ttfamily true} if the current source buffer is the last available chunk of the source, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. Note that if a failing status is returned, this function may have to be called multiple times with flush set to {\ttfamily true} until the source buffer is consumed. \\
\hline
{\em err} & the error status. {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+I\+L\+L\+E\+G\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} will be set if the converter is {\ttfamily N\+U\+LL}. {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} will be set if the target is full and there is still data to be written to the target. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ucnv\_usesFallback()}{ucnv\_usesFallback()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 ucnv\+\_\+uses\+Fallback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{ucnv__err_8h_a0c2dcfbf71ad577f5285869e1ceb26b1}{U\+Converter}} $\ast$}]{cnv }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}
